				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Liebster Gott, wenn werd ich sterben?, BWV 8 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Liebster Gott, wenn werd ich sterben?
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Beloved God, when will I die?
</td></tr>

<th>Name Translations

</td></tr>

</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: Liebster Gott, wenn werd ich sterben? (E&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Was willst du dich, mein Geist, entsetzen (C<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span>&#160;minor)
</li><li>Recitative (alto): Zwar fühlt mein schwaches Herz (E&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (bass): Doch weichet, ihr tollen, vergeblichen Sorgen! (A&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitative (soprano): Behalte nur, o Welt, das Meine! (E&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale: Herrscher über Tod und Leben (E&#160;major)
</li></ol>

</li></ul>
